2. Backend — File-by-File Responsibilities
2.1 server.js
🤖  Entry point. Sets up Express, mounts all middleware and routes. No business logic here.

// server.js
require('dotenv').config();
const express   = require('express');
const cors      = require('cors');
const connectDB = require('./config/db');

connectDB();

const app = express();

// ── Core Middleware ──────────────────────────────────────────
app.use(cors({ origin: process.env.CLIENT_URL, credentials: true }));
app.use(express.json());

// ── Routes ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
app.use('/api/auth',            require('./routes/authRoutes'));
app.use('/api/users',           require('./routes/userRoutes'));
app.use('/api/gemstones',       require('./routes/gemstoneRoutes'));
app.use('/api/recommendations', require('./routes/recommendationRoutes'));
app.use('/api/admin',           require('./routes/adminRoutes'));

// ── Global Error Handler (must be last) ─────────────────────
app.use(require('./middleware/errorHandler'));

const PORT = process.env.PORT || 5000;
app.listen(PORT, () => console.log(`✅ Server running on port ${PORT}`));


2.2 config/db.js

// config/db.js
const mongoose = require('mongoose');

const connectDB = async () => {
  try {
    await mongoose.connect(process.env.MONGODB_URI);
    console.log('✅ MongoDB connected');
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('❌ MongoDB connection failed:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  }
};

module.exports = connectDB;


2.3 middleware/auth.js
🤖  Two exported functions: protect (verify JWT, attach req.user) and adminOnly (check role). Both used as route middleware.

// middleware/auth.js
const jwt  = require('jsonwebtoken');
const User = require('../models/User');

// Attach authenticated user to req.user
exports.protect = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const header = req.headers.authorization;
    if (!header || !header.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
      return res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'Not authenticated' });
    }
    const token   = header.split(' ')[1];
    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET);
    req.user = await User.findById(decoded.id);
    if (!req.user) return res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'User not found' });
    next();
  } catch {
    return res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'Invalid or expired token' });
  }
};

// Must follow protect in middleware chain
exports.adminOnly = (req, res, next) => {
  if (req.user?.role !== 'admin') {
    return res.status(403).json({ success: false, message: 'Admin access required' });
  }
  next();
};


2.4 middleware/errorHandler.js

// middleware/errorHandler.js
// Catches any error passed via next(err) or unhandled throws
module.exports = (err, req, res, next) => {
  console.error(err.stack);
  const status = err.statusCode || 500;
  res.status(status).json({
    success: false,
    message: err.message || 'Internal server error'
  });
};

3. Controller Skeletons — All 15 Endpoints
3.1 authController.js
💡  Handles POST /auth/register and POST /auth/login. Generates JWT with 7d expiry.

// controllers/authController.js
const jwt  = require('jsonwebtoken');
const User = require('../models/User');

// Helper — sign token
const signToken = (id) =>
  jwt.sign({ id }, process.env.JWT_SECRET, { expiresIn: '7d' });

// ── POST /api/auth/register ─────────────────────────────────
// Validation: name required, email unique, password min 6 chars
// zodiacSign must be one of 12 valid signs, birthMonth 1-12
exports.register = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const { name, email, password, zodiacSign, birthMonth, preference } = req.body;

    // 1. Validate required fields
    if (!name || !email || !password) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'name, email and password are required' });
    }

    // 2. Check email not already taken
    const existing = await User.findOne({ email: email.toLowerCase() });
    if (existing) return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Email already registered' });

    // 3. Create user (password hashed by pre-save hook)
    const user = await User.create({ name, email, password, zodiacSign, birthMonth, preference });

    // 4. Sign and return token
    const token = signToken(user._id);
    res.status(201).json({
      success: true, token,
      user: { _id:user._id, name:user.name, email:user.email,
              role:user.role, zodiacSign:user.zodiacSign,
              birthMonth:user.birthMonth, preference:user.preference }
    });
  } catch (err) { next(err); }
};

// ── POST /api/auth/login ─────────────────────────────────────
// Validation: email + password required
exports.login = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const { email, password } = req.body;
    if (!email || !password) return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Email and password required' });

    // select(+password) because password has select:false in schema
    const user = await User.findOne({ email: email.toLowerCase() }).select('+password');
    if (!user) return res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' });

    const match = await user.matchPassword(password);
    if (!match) return res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' });

    const token = signToken(user._id);
    res.json({
      success: true, token,
      user: { _id:user._id, name:user.name, email:user.email,
              role:user.role, zodiacSign:user.zodiacSign,
              birthMonth:user.birthMonth, preference:user.preference }
    });
  } catch (err) { next(err); }
};


3.2 userController.js
💡  GET /api/users/me returns profile. PUT /api/users/me updates zodiacSign, birthMonth, preference, name only.

// controllers/userController.js
const User = require('../models/User');

// ── GET /api/users/me ────────────────────────────────────────
// Auth: protect
// Returns: user object (no password)
exports.getMe = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    res.json({ success: true, user: req.user });
  } catch (err) { next(err); }
};

// ── PUT /api/users/me ────────────────────────────────────────
// Auth: protect
// Allowed fields: name, zodiacSign, birthMonth, preference
// Validation: zodiacSign must be valid enum, birthMonth 1-12
exports.updateMe = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const allowed = ['name', 'zodiacSign', 'birthMonth', 'preference'];
    const updates = {};
    allowed.forEach(field => { if (req.body[field] !== undefined) updates[field] = req.body[field]; });

    const user = await User.findByIdAndUpdate(
      req.user._id,
      updates,
      { new: true, runValidators: true }
    );
    res.json({ success: true, user });
  } catch (err) { next(err); }
};


3.3 gemstoneController.js
💡  List+Search (public), Detail (public), Create/Update/Delete (admin only).

// controllers/gemstoneController.js
const Gemstone = require('../models/Gemstone');

// ── GET /api/gemstones  (?q=searchTerm) ─────────────────────
// Auth: public
// Query params: q (string) — searches name and description
// Returns: array of all active gemstones (or filtered)
exports.getAll = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const filter = {};
    if (req.query.q) {
      const re = new RegExp(req.query.q, 'i');
      filter.$or = [{ name: re }, { description: re }, { category: re }, { color: re }];
    }
    const gemstones = await Gemstone.find(filter).sort({ name: 1 });
    res.json({ success: true, count: gemstones.length, gemstones });
  } catch (err) { next(err); }
};

// ── GET /api/gemstones/:id ───────────────────────────────────
// Auth: public
exports.getOne = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const gem = await Gemstone.findById(req.params.id);
    if (!gem) return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: 'Gemstone not found' });
    res.json({ success: true, gemstone: gem });
  } catch (err) { next(err); }
};

// ── POST /api/gemstones ──────────────────────────────────────
// Auth: protect + adminOnly
// Body: name*, description*, category*, color*, zodiacSigns[], birthMonths[], imageUrl, price, inStock
// Validation: name unique, category must be valid enum
exports.create = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const { name, description, category, color, zodiacSigns,
            birthMonths, imageUrl, price, inStock } = req.body;
    if (!name || !description || !category || !color) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'name, description, category, color required' });
    }
    const gem = await Gemstone.create({ name, description, category, color,
      zodiacSigns: zodiacSigns || [], birthMonths: birthMonths || [],
      imageUrl: imageUrl || '', price: price || 0,
      inStock: inStock !== undefined ? inStock : true });
    res.status(201).json({ success: true, gemstone: gem });
  } catch (err) { next(err); }
};

// ── PUT /api/gemstones/:id ───────────────────────────────────
// Auth: protect + adminOnly
// Body: any subset of gemstone fields
exports.update = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const gem = await Gemstone.findByIdAndUpdate(req.params.id, req.body,
      { new: true, runValidators: true });
    if (!gem) return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: 'Gemstone not found' });
    res.json({ success: true, gemstone: gem });
  } catch (err) { next(err); }
};

// ── DELETE /api/gemstones/:id ────────────────────────────────
// Auth: protect + adminOnly
exports.remove = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const gem = await Gemstone.findByIdAndDelete(req.params.id);
    if (!gem) return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: 'Gemstone not found' });
    res.json({ success: true, message: 'Gemstone deleted' });
  } catch (err) { next(err); }
};


3.4 recommendationController.js
💡  generate runs the 3-level fallback engine and saves history. history returns paginated past results. remove deletes one entry.

// controllers/recommendationController.js
const Gemstone       = require('../models/Gemstone');
const Recommendation = require('../models/Recommendation');
const ZODIAC_GEMS    = require('../data/recommendationMap');

// ── POST /api/recommendations/generate ──────────────────────
// Auth: protect
// Body: zodiacSign*, birthMonth*, preference*
// Validation: zodiacSign must exist in ZODIAC_GEMS map
exports.generate = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const { zodiacSign, birthMonth, preference } = req.body;
    if (!zodiacSign || !birthMonth || !preference) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'zodiacSign, birthMonth, preference required' });
    }

    const names = ZODIAC_GEMS[zodiacSign];
    if (!names) return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Invalid zodiac sign' });

    // Level 1: all 3 criteria
    let results = await Gemstone.find({
      name: { $in: names }, birthMonths: Number(birthMonth),
      category: preference, inStock: true
    }).limit(5);

    // Level 2: zodiac + preference
    if (results.length < 3) {
      results = await Gemstone.find({
        name: { $in: names }, category: preference, inStock: true
      }).limit(5);
    }

    // Level 3: zodiac only
    if (results.length < 3) {
      results = await Gemstone.find({ name: { $in: names }, inStock: true }).limit(5);
    }

    const rec = await Recommendation.create({
      userId: req.user._id, zodiacSign, birthMonth: Number(birthMonth),
      preference, gemstones: results.map(g => g._id)
    });

    res.json({ success: true, recommendationId: rec._id, gemstones: results });
  } catch (err) { next(err); }
};

// ── GET /api/recommendations/history ────────────────────────
// Auth: protect
// Returns: last 20 recommendations for req.user, newest first
exports.history = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const recs = await Recommendation.find({ userId: req.user._id })
      .populate('gemstones', 'name color category imageUrl price')
      .sort({ createdAt: -1 })
      .limit(20);
    res.json({ success: true, recommendations: recs });
  } catch (err) { next(err); }
};

// ── DELETE /api/recommendations/:id ─────────────────────────
// Auth: protect
// Only owner can delete their own recommendation
exports.remove = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const rec = await Recommendation.findOneAndDelete({
      _id: req.params.id, userId: req.user._id
    });
    if (!rec) return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: 'Not found' });
    res.json({ success: true, message: 'Deleted' });
  } catch (err) { next(err); }
};


3.5 adminController.js
💡  All admin routes require protect + adminOnly in the middleware chain.

// controllers/adminController.js
const User           = require('../models/User');
const Gemstone       = require('../models/Gemstone');
const Recommendation = require('../models/Recommendation');

// ── GET /api/admin/stats ─────────────────────────────────────
exports.getStats = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const [totalUsers, totalGemstones, totalRecommendations, topZodiac] = await Promise.all([
      User.countDocuments({ role: 'user' }),
      Gemstone.countDocuments(),
      Recommendation.countDocuments(),
      Recommendation.aggregate([
        { $group: { _id: '$zodiacSign', count: { $sum: 1 } } },
        { $sort:  { count: -1 } },
        { $limit: 1 }
      ])
    ]);
    res.json({
      success: true,
      stats: {
        totalUsers,
        totalGemstones,
        totalRecommendations,
        mostPopularZodiac: topZodiac[0]?._id || 'N/A'
      }
    });
  } catch (err) { next(err); }
};

// ── GET /api/admin/users ─────────────────────────────────────
// Returns all users excluding passwords, sorted by createdAt desc
exports.getUsers = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const users = await User.find().sort({ createdAt: -1 });
    res.json({ success: true, count: users.length, users });
  } catch (err) { next(err); }
};

// ── DELETE /api/admin/users/:id ──────────────────────────────
// Prevent deleting own account or other admins
exports.deleteUser = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    if (req.params.id === req.user._id.toString()) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Cannot delete your own account' });
    }
    const user = await User.findByIdAndDelete(req.params.id);
    if (!user) return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: 'User not found' });
    res.json({ success: true, message: 'User deleted' });
  } catch (err) { next(err); }
};

4. Route Skeletons
4.1 routes/authRoutes.js

const router = require('express').Router();
const { register, login } = require('../controllers/authController');

router.post('/register', register);
router.post('/login',    login);

module.exports = router;


4.2 routes/userRoutes.js

const router              = require('express').Router();
const { protect }         = require('../middleware/auth');
const { getMe, updateMe } = require('../controllers/userController');

router.get('/',  protect, getMe);
router.put('/',  protect, updateMe);

// Mounted at /api/users → GET /api/users/me and PUT /api/users/me
// Note: routes are mounted at /api/users, so path is just /

module.exports = router;

💡  In server.js the mount is app.use("/api/users", userRoutes). So router path "/" becomes GET /api/users/me equivalent. You can also use /me as the path — just keep consistent with the frontend API calls.

4.3 routes/gemstoneRoutes.js

const router                              = require('express').Router();
const { protect, adminOnly }              = require('../middleware/auth');
const { getAll, getOne, create,
        update, remove }                  = require('../controllers/gemstoneController');

// Public
router.get('/',     getAll);
router.get('/:id',  getOne);

// Admin only
router.post('/',     protect, adminOnly, create);
router.put('/:id',   protect, adminOnly, update);
router.delete('/:id',protect, adminOnly, remove);

module.exports = router;


4.4 routes/recommendationRoutes.js

const router                          = require('express').Router();
const { protect }                     = require('../middleware/auth');
const { generate, history, remove }   = require('../controllers/recommendationController');

router.post('/generate',  protect, generate);
router.get('/history',    protect, history);
router.delete('/:id',     protect, remove);

module.exports = router;


4.5 routes/adminRoutes.js

const router                              = require('express').Router();
const { protect, adminOnly }              = require('../middleware/auth');
const { getStats, getUsers,
        deleteUser }                      = require('../controllers/adminController');

// All admin routes require both middleware
router.get('/stats',       protect, adminOnly, getStats);
router.get('/users',       protect, adminOnly, getUsers);
router.delete('/users/:id',protect, adminOnly, deleteUser);

module.exports = router;

5. Frontend — File-by-File Responsibilities
5.1 src/api/axios.js
🤖  Single Axios instance used by ALL pages. Never create a second axios instance or import axios directly in pages.

// src/api/axios.js
import axios from 'axios';

const API = axios.create({
  baseURL: import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL || 'http://localhost:5000/api',
});

// Attach JWT to every outgoing request
API.interceptors.request.use(config => {
  const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
  if (token) config.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${token}`;
  return config;
});

export default API;


5.2 src/context/AuthContext.jsx
🤖  Global auth state. user and token are initialized from localStorage so the session survives a page refresh.

import { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect } from 'react';

export const AuthContext = createContext(null);

export function AuthProvider({ children }) {
  const [user,  setUser]  = useState(null);
  const [token, setToken] = useState(localStorage.getItem('token'));

  useEffect(() => {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem('user');
    if (saved) setUser(JSON.parse(saved));
  }, []);

  const login = (userData, jwt) => {
    setUser(userData); setToken(jwt);
    localStorage.setItem('user',  JSON.stringify(userData));
    localStorage.setItem('token', jwt);
  };

  const logout = () => {
    setUser(null); setToken(null);
    localStorage.removeItem('user');
    localStorage.removeItem('token');
  };

  // Call this after profile update to keep localStorage in sync
  const updateUser = (updated) => {
    setUser(updated);
    localStorage.setItem('user', JSON.stringify(updated));
  };

  return (
    <AuthContext.Provider value={{ user, token, login, logout, updateUser }}>
      {children}
    </AuthContext.Provider>
  );
}

export const useAuth = () => useContext(AuthContext);


5.3 src/components/ProtectedRoute.jsx

import { Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useAuth }  from '../context/AuthContext';

export default function ProtectedRoute({ children }) {
  const { token } = useAuth();
  return token ? children : <Navigate to='/login' replace />;
}


5.4 src/components/AdminRoute.jsx

import { Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useAuth }  from '../context/AuthContext';

export default function AdminRoute({ children }) {
  const { user, token } = useAuth();
  if (!token) return <Navigate to='/login' replace />;
  if (user?.role !== 'admin') return <Navigate to='/' replace />;
  return children;
}


5.5 src/components/GemstoneCard.jsx
💡  Accepts a gemstone prop. onEdit and onDelete are optional — only passed by the Admin Dashboard.

export default function GemstoneCard({ gemstone, onEdit, onDelete }) {
  const { name, color, category, imageUrl, price, description } = gemstone;
  return (
    <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-md overflow-hidden hover:shadow-lg transition">
      <img src={imageUrl || 'https://via.placeholder.com/300x200?text=Gemstone'}
           alt={name} className="w-full h-44 object-cover" />
      <div className="p-4">
        <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-1">
          <h3 className="font-bold text-lg text-slate-800">{name}</h3>
          <span className="text-xs bg-emerald-100 text-emerald-700 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full capitalize">
            {category}
          </span>
        </div>
        <p className="text-xs text-slate-500 mb-2">{color}</p>
        <p className="text-sm text-slate-600 line-clamp-2">{description}</p>
        <p className="mt-3 font-semibold text-slate-800">₹{price}</p>
        {(onEdit || onDelete) && (
          <div className="flex gap-2 mt-3">
            {onEdit   && <button onClick={() => onEdit(gemstone)}
                                 className="flex-1 text-sm py-1 bg-blue-50 text-blue-600 rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-100">Edit</button>}
            {onDelete && <button onClick={() => onDelete(gemstone._id)}
                                 className="flex-1 text-sm py-1 bg-red-50 text-red-600 rounded-lg hover:bg-red-100">Delete</button>}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

5.7 src/components/Navbar.jsx
💡  Shows different links based on auth state. Admin sees an "Admin" link. Logout clears context and redirects to /.

import { Link, useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useAuth } from '../context/AuthContext';

export default function Navbar() {
  const { user, token, logout } = useAuth();
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  const handleLogout = () => { logout(); navigate('/'); };

  return (
    <nav className="bg-white shadow-sm sticky top-0 z-50">
      <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto px-4 py-3 flex justify-between items-center">
        <Link to="/" className="text-xl font-bold text-blue-700">💎 GemStone</Link>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-4 text-sm font-medium">
          <Link to="/catalog" className="text-slate-600 hover:text-blue-600">Catalog</Link>
          {token ? (
            <>
              <Link to="/recommend" className="text-slate-600 hover:text-blue-600">Recommend</Link>
              <Link to="/history"   className="text-slate-600 hover:text-blue-600">History</Link>
              <Link to="/profile"   className="text-slate-600 hover:text-blue-600">Profile</Link>
              {user?.role === 'admin' && <Link to="/admin" className="text-violet-600 hover:text-violet-800">Admin</Link>}
              <button onClick={handleLogout} className="bg-red-50 text-red-600 px-3 py-1 rounded-lg hover:bg-red-100">Logout</button>
            </>
          ) : (
            <>
              <Link to="/login"    className="text-slate-600 hover:text-blue-600">Login</Link>
              <Link to="/register" className="bg-blue-600 text-white px-4 py-1.5 rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-700">Register</Link>
            </>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </nav>
  );
}

6.1 Home Page  (pages/Home.jsx)
Wireframe
<w:left w:val="single" w:color="CBD5E1" w:sz="1"/><w:right w:val="single" w:color="CBD5E1" w:sz="1"/></w:pBdr><w:shd w:fill="F1F5F9" w:val="clear"/><w:spacing w:after="0" w:before="100"/></w:pPr><w:r><w:t xml:space="preserve">
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  NAVBAR: Logo | Catalog | Login | Register              │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                         │
│     💎  Discover Your Perfect Gemstone                  │
│     Find gems aligned with your zodiac, birth month     │
│     and personal energy.                                │
│                                                         │
│     [ Get My Recommendation ]  [ Browse Catalog ]       │
│                                                         │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  WHY GEMSTONES?  |  HOW IT WORKS  |  POPULAR STONES     │
│  3 icon cards with short descriptions                   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

State Variables

// No state — static page. Uses useAuth() to route CTA button correctly.

Component Hierarchy

Home
  └── Navbar (shared)
  └── HeroSection
        ├── <Link to="/recommend"> OR <Link to="/register">  (based on token)
        └── <Link to="/catalog">
  └── FeatureCards  (3 static info cards)

Key Implementation Notes
CTA button: if token exists, link to /recommend; else link to /register
No API calls — pure static content
Tailwind: min-h-screen flex flex-col on the hero section

6.2 Login Page  (pages/Login.jsx)
Wireframe
<w:left w:val="single" w:color="CBD5E1" w:sz="1"/><w:right w:val="single" w:color="CBD5E1" w:sz="1"/></w:pBdr><w:shd w:fill="F1F5F9" w:val="clear"/><w:spacing w:after="0" w:before="100"/></w:pPr><w:r><w:t xml:space="preserve">
┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  NAVBAR                                  │
├──────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                          │
│    ┌────────────────────────────────┐    │
│    │  💎 Sign In                    │    │
│    │                                │    │
│    │  Email ________________________│    │
│    │  Password ____________________│    │
│    │                                │    │
│    │  [   Sign In   ]  (loading...) │    │
│    │                                │    │
│    │  ⚠ Error message (if any)      │    │
│    │                                │    │
│    │  Don't have an account?         │    │
│    │  → Register here               │    │
│    └────────────────────────────────┘    │
│                                          │
└──────────────────────────────────────────┘

State Variables

const [email,    setEmail]    = useState('');
const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
const [loading,  setLoading]  = useState(false);
const [error,    setError]    = useState('');

API Call

// On form submit:
const res = await API.post('/auth/login', { email, password });
// On success: login(res.data.user, res.data.token) → navigate("/recommend")
// On error:   setError(err.response?.data?.message || "Login failed")

Component Hierarchy

Login
  └── Navbar
  └── Card (centered div)
        ├── <form onSubmit={handleLogin}>
        │     ├── <input type="email">
        │     ├── <input type="password">
        │     └── <button type="submit"> {loading ? "Signing in..." : "Sign In"}
        ├── Error message div (conditional)
        └── <Link to="/register">


6.3 Register Page  (pages/Register.jsx)
Wireframe
<w:left w:val="single" w:color="CBD5E1" w:sz="1"/><w:right w:val="single" w:color="CBD5E1" w:sz="1"/></w:pBdr><w:shd w:fill="F1F5F9" w:val="clear"/><w:spacing w:after="0" w:before="100"/></w:pPr><w:r><w:t xml:space="preserve">
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  NAVBAR                                      │
├──────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │  💎 Create Account                   │   │
│  │                                      │   │
│  │  Name _______________________________│   │
│  │  Email ______________________________│   │
│  │  Password ___________________________│   │
│  │                                      │   │
│  │  Zodiac Sign  [dropdown ▼]            │   │
│  │  Birth Month  [1–12 number input]     │   │
│  │  Preference   [dropdown ▼]            │   │
│  │                                      │   │
│  │  [   Create Account   ]              │   │
│  │  ⚠ Error message                    │   │
│  │                                      │   │
│  │  Already have an account? → Login    │   │
│  └──────────────────────────────────────┘   │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────┘

State Variables

const [form, setForm] = useState({
  name: '', email: '', password: '',
  zodiacSign: '', birthMonth: '', preference: 'healing'
});
const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
const [error,   setError]   = useState('');

Dropdown Values

const ZODIACS = ['Aries','Taurus','Gemini','Cancer','Leo','Virgo',
                 'Libra','Scorpio','Sagittarius','Capricorn','Aquarius','Pisces'];
const PREFS   = ['healing','protection','wealth','love','clarity','energy'];

API Call

const res = await API.post('/auth/register', form);
// On success: login(res.data.user, res.data.token) → navigate("/recommend")


6.4 Catalog Page  (pages/Catalog.jsx)
Wireframe
<w:left w:val="single" w:color="CBD5E1" w:sz="1"/><w:right w:val="single" w:color="CBD5E1" w:sz="1"/></w:pBdr><w:shd w:fill="F1F5F9" w:val="clear"/><w:spacing w:after="0" w:before="100"/></w:pPr><w:r><w:t xml:space="preserve">
┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  NAVBAR                                                    │
├────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  Gemstone Catalog                                          │
│  [ 🔍 Search name, color, category...        ] [Search]   │
│                                                            │
│  Showing 20 gemstones  (or "X results for 'ruby'")         │
│                                                            │
│  ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐     │
│  │  [img]   │ │  [img]   │ │  [img]   │ │  [img]   │     │
│  │ Amethyst │ │  Ruby    │ │ Emerald  │ │ Sapphire │     │
│  │ Violet   │ │ Red      │ │ Green    │ │ Blue     │     │
│  │ healing  │ │ energy   │ │ love     │ │ clarity  │     │
│  │ ₹850     │ │ ₹3200    │ │ ₹4500    │ │ ₹5500    │     │
│  └──────────┘ └──────────┘ └──────────┘ └──────────┘     │
│  ... (grid continues, 4 cols desktop / 2 cols mobile)     │
└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

State Variables

const [gemstones, setGemstones] = useState([]);
const [search,    setSearch]    = useState('');
const [loading,   setLoading]   = useState(true);

API Calls

// On mount and on search submit:
const res = await API.get(`/gemstones${search ? `?q=${search}` : ''}`);
setGemstones(res.data.gemstones);

Component Hierarchy

Catalog
  └── Navbar
  └── SearchBar  (<input> + <button>)
  └── Loader  (conditional)
  └── Results count text
  └── Grid div (grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4)
        └── GemstoneCard[]  (no onEdit/onDelete props)

Search Behavior
Search fires on button click OR on Enter key press
Empty search string fetches all gemstones (GET /gemstones with no query)
Debounce is NOT required for this project — button-triggered search is fine

6.5 Recommend Page  (pages/Recommend.jsx)
Wireframe
<w:left w:val="single" w:color="CBD5E1" w:sz="1"/><w:right w:val="single" w:color="CBD5E1" w:sz="1"/></w:pBdr><w:shd w:fill="F1F5F9" w:val="clear"/><w:spacing w:after="0" w:before="100"/></w:pPr><w:r><w:t xml:space="preserve">
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  NAVBAR                                                  │
├──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  Get Your Gemstone Recommendation                        │
│                                                          │
│  ┌────────────────────────────────────────────────┐     │
│  │  Zodiac Sign    [Scorpio             ▼]         │     │
│  │  Birth Month    [11                    ]        │     │
│  │  Preference     [healing             ▼]         │     │
│  │  (pre-filled from profile if available)         │     │
│  │                                                  │     │
│  │  [ ✨ Get My Recommendations ]                   │     │
│  └────────────────────────────────────────────────┘     │
│                                                          │
│  ── Your Recommended Gemstones ──────────────────────    │
│                                                          │
│  ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐               │
│  │  Amethyst│ │Blk Tour..│ │  Topaz   │               │
│  │ healing  │ │protection│ │ wealth   │               │
│  │  ₹850    │ │  ₹600    │ │  ₹1200   │               │
│  └──────────┘ └──────────┘ └──────────┘               │
│  Saved to your history ✓                               │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

State Variables

// Form is pre-filled from user profile
const [form, setForm] = useState({
  zodiacSign: user?.zodiacSign || '',
  birthMonth: user?.birthMonth || '',
  preference: user?.preference || 'healing'
});
const [results,   setResults]   = useState([]);
const [loading,   setLoading]   = useState(false);
const [submitted, setSubmitted] = useState(false);
const [error,     setError]     = useState('');

API Call

const res = await API.post('/recommendations/generate', form);
setResults(res.data.gemstones);
setSubmitted(true);

Component Hierarchy

Recommend
  └── Navbar
  └── RecommendForm
        ├── Zodiac dropdown (ZODIACS array)
        ├── Birth month input (type=number, min=1, max=12)
        └── Preference dropdown (PREFS array)
  └── Loader (while loading)
  └── Results section (if submitted && results.length)
        └── GemstoneCard[] (results array)
  └── Empty state (if submitted && results.length === 0)


6.6 History Page  (pages/History.jsx)
Wireframe
<w:left w:val="single" w:color="CBD5E1" w:sz="1"/><w:right w:val="single" w:color="CBD5E1" w:sz="1"/></w:pBdr><w:shd w:fill="F1F5F9" w:val="clear"/><w:spacing w:after="0" w:before="100"/></w:pPr><w:r><w:t xml:space="preserve">
┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  NAVBAR                                                │
├────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  My Recommendation History                             │
│                                                        │

│  Scorpio · Month 11 · healing                         │
│  ┌────────┐ ┌──────────┐ ┌────────┐                  │
│  │Amethyst│ │Blk Tour. │ │ Topaz  │                  │
│  └────────┘ └──────────┘ └────────┘                  │
│  [ 🗑 Delete this entry ]                              │
│                                                        │

State Variables

const [recs,    setRecs]    = useState([]);
const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

API Calls

// On mount:
const res = await API.get('/recommendations/history');
setRecs(res.data.recommendations);

// On delete:
await API.delete(`/recommendations/${id}`);
setRecs(prev => prev.filter(r => r._id !== id));   // optimistic UI

Component Hierarchy

History
  └── Navbar
  └── Loader (if loading)
  └── Empty state (if recs.length === 0)
  └── recs.map(rec =>
        RecommendationEntry
          ├── Date + zodiac/month/preference summary line
          ├── GemstoneCard[] (rec.gemstones — populated from API)
          └── Delete button → calls handleDelete(rec._id)

// Initialize from user context

6.8 Admin Dashboard  (pages/admin/Dashboard.jsx)
🤖  Single-page admin with tabbed sections: Overview | Gemstones | Users. All in one file.
Wireframe
<w:left w:val="single" w:color="CBD5E1" w:sz="1"/><w:right w:val="single" w:color="CBD5E1" w:sz="1"/></w:pBdr><w:shd w:fill="F1F5F9" w:val="clear"/><w:spacing w:after="0" w:before="100"/></w:pPr><w:r><w:t xml:space="preserve">
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  NAVBAR  (Admin badge visible)                               │
├──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  Admin Dashboard                                             │
│                                                              │
│  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐   │
│  │  Users   │  │ Gemstones│  │  Recs    │  │ Top Sign │   │
│  │    42    │  │    20    │  │   138    │  │ Scorpio  │   │
│  └──────────┘  └──────────┘  └──────────┘  └──────────┘   │
│                                                              │
│  [ Overview ] [ Gemstones ] [ Users ]    ← Tab buttons      │
│                                                              │
│  ── GEMSTONES TAB ───────────────────────────────────────   │
│  [ + Add Gemstone ]                                          │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │ Name          │ Category  │ Price │ Stock │ Actions  │   │
│  │ Amethyst      │ healing   │ ₹850  │  ✓    │ Edit Del │   │
│  │ Ruby          │ energy    │ ₹3200 │  ✓    │ Edit Del │   │
│  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
│                                                              │
│  ── MODAL: Add/Edit Gemstone form ─────────────────────     │
│  [ Name ] [ Description ] [ Category ▼ ] [ Color ]          │
│  [ Zodiac Signs (multi) ] [ Birth Months ] [ Price ]         │
│  [ Image URL ] [ In Stock ✓ ]                                │
│  [ Save ]  [ Cancel ]                                        │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

State Variables

const [activeTab,  setActiveTab]  = useState('overview');  // 'overview'|'gemstones'|'users'
const [stats,      setStats]      = useState(null);
const [gemstones,  setGemstones]  = useState([]);
const [users,      setUsers]      = useState([]);
const [loading,    setLoading]    = useState(true);

// Modal state
const [showModal,  setShowModal]  = useState(false);
const [editTarget, setEditTarget] = useState(null);  // null = create, object = edit
const [gemForm, setGemForm] = useState({
  name:'', description:'', category:'healing', color:'',
  zodiacSigns:[], birthMonths:[], imageUrl:'', price:0, inStock:true
});

API Calls

// On mount (fetch everything in parallel):
const [statsRes, gemsRes, usersRes] = await Promise.all([
  API.get('/admin/stats'),
  API.get('/gemstones'),
  API.get('/admin/users')
]);

// Create gemstone:
await API.post('/gemstones', gemForm);

// Update gemstone:
await API.put(`/gemstones/${editTarget._id}`, gemForm);

// Delete gemstone:
await API.delete(`/gemstones/${id}`);
setGemstones(prev => prev.filter(g => g._id !== id));

// Delete user:
await API.delete(`/admin/users/${id}`);
setUsers(prev => prev.filter(u => u._id !== id));

Component Hierarchy (all in one file)

Dashboard
  └── Navbar
  └── StatsRow
        └── StatCard × 4  (Users, Gemstones, Recs, Top Zodiac)
  └── TabBar  (3 buttons, sets activeTab)
  └── {activeTab === "gemstones" &&
        GemstonesPanel
          ├── AddButton → opens modal with editTarget=null
          ├── GemstoneTable
          │     └── row × n  (name, category, price, inStock, Edit/Delete buttons)
          └── GemstoneModal  (conditionally rendered)
                ├── form inputs for all fields
                ├── Save button → create or update
                └── Cancel button → closes modal
      }
  └── {activeTab === "users" &&
        UsersPanel
          └── UserTable
                └── row × n  (name, email, zodiac, role, Delete button)
      }

8. Configuration Files
8.1 server/.env (template)

PORT=5000
MONGODB_URI=mongodb+srv://<user>:<pass>@cluster0.mongodb.net/gemstone_db?retryWrites=true&w=majority
JWT_SECRET=replace_this_with_a_32_char_random_string_abc123
CLIENT_URL=http://localhost:5173


8.2 server/package.json

{
  "name": "gemstone-server",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "main": "server.js",
  "scripts": {
    "start":  "node server.js",
    "dev":    "nodemon server.js"
  },
  "dependencies": {
    "bcryptjs":     "^2.4.3",
    "cors":         "^2.8.5",
    "dotenv":       "^16.3.1",
    "express":      "^4.18.2",
    "jsonwebtoken": "^9.0.0",
    "mongoose":     "^7.5.0"
  },
  "devDependencies": {
    "nodemon": "^3.0.1"
  }
}

# Development
VITE_API_URL=http://localhost:5000/api

# Production (replace with your Render URL)
# VITE_API_URL=https://gemstone-api.onrender.com/api

    </AuthProvider>
  </React.StrictMode>
);

9.4 Postman Test Sequence
Run these in order to verify the entire backend before starting the frontend:

1. POST /api/auth/register        → save token as {{token}}
2. POST /api/auth/login           → confirm same token returned
3. GET  /api/users/me             → Bearer {{token}}
4. PUT  /api/users/me             → update zodiacSign to "Scorpio"
5. GET  /api/gemstones            → should return 20 seeded gems
6. GET  /api/gemstones?q=amethyst → should return 1 gem
7. GET  /api/gemstones/:id        → use any _id from step 5
8. [set role to admin in Atlas]
9. POST /api/auth/login           → re-login to get fresh user object
10. POST /api/gemstones           → create a test gemstone
11. PUT  /api/gemstones/:id       → edit the test gemstone
12. DELETE /api/gemstones/:id     → delete the test gemstone
13. POST /api/recommendations/generate → body: {zodiacSign:"Scorpio",birthMonth:11,preference:"healing"}
14. GET  /api/recommendations/history
15. DELETE /api/recommendations/:id
16. GET  /api/admin/stats
17. GET  /api/admin/users
18. DELETE /api/admin/users/:id  → use a test user ID

— End of Implementation Blueprint —
